#  No one knows Africa like we do
As a leader in African capital markets with a comprehensive suite of products, we have a unique ability to leverage our local presence and global reach

* * *

###  OUR EXPERTISE 
#  No one knows Africa like we do 
[Absa | Corporate and Investment Banking](https://cib.absa.africa "Go to Absa | Corporate and Investment Banking.") > About Us
##  We stand with you to make your vision a reality 
###  With a relentless African spirit and distinct client focus, we have become a leading corporate and investment bank in and for our continent. 
![medium-liq-opt-copy](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/medium-liq-opt-copy-1.jpg)
Tag
###  150 years of African heritage 
####  Beyond our company ethos and our wealth of experience, our bravery to imagine and our will to get it done makes us the right partner to bring your African vision to life. 
With over one and a half centuries of experience – and a significant footprint across the continent – we are a proudly pan-African institution that believes in building courageous partnerships that work.
In doing so, we go to extraordinary lengths to exceed expectations. We challenge limits and close distances, connecting people to opportunities across borders, languages and cultures.
Because African ingenuity knows no boundaries, neither do we.
###  A truly pan-African bank 
####  We’re a forward-thinking African business with a local presence in 10 countries across the continent, making us ideally positioned to solve regional challenges. 
Absa Group Limited is a listed, diversified financial services provider headquartered in Johannesburg, South Africa.
With an extensive branch network, a team of 41 000 banking professionals and a customer base of over 12 million, we are one of Africa’s most respected banks.
Our presence on the continent includes regionally-coordinated coverage in 12 markets with on-the-ground banking capabilities in Botswana, Ghana, Kenya, Mauritius, Mozambique, Seychelles, South Africa, Tanzania, Uganda and Zambia – and representative offices in Namibia and Nigeria.
We provide global reach through our international offices situated in London and New York.
![ABOUT-Card2-A-Truly-Pan-African-Bank-617x579-Filtered20](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/ABOUT-Card2-A-Truly-Pan-African-Bank-617x579-Filtered20.jpg)
![flags](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/flags.jpg)
Tag
###  Driving business in Africa with international expertise and local knowledge 
####  Our recent Memorandum of understanding and detailed cooperation agreement with Societe Generale (SocGen)leverages global expertise that enables us to drive connectivity across key client corridors of UK/Europe, US & China, into and within Africa. 
With shared ambitions on the continent, our aligned innovative approach enables us to better serve clients, both local and international, in their banking needs across the continent.
We're taking business to more of Africa than ever before.
[ Learn More ](https://cib.absa.africa/about-us/taking-business-to-more-of-africa-than-ever-before/)
###  Our capabilities and expertise 
####  Our Corporate and [Investment Banking](https://cib.absa.africa/) business is a leader in African capital markets and offers a comprehensive suite of products, with the ability to leverage a unique combination of local presence and global reach. 
Turning an investment opportunity in Africa into something exceptional requires a financial services partner on your doorstep who can offer universal solutions to meet your business needs.
Our industry leaders work in Africa’s key sectors to bring possibilities to life across a comprehensive suite of corporate and investment banking services.
As one of Africa's largest listed banking groups, we harness our deep understanding of investment flows, market participants, sector trends and regulations to unlock value for our clients across the continent.
![ABOUT-Card3-Our-Capabilities-And-Expertise-Filtered20](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/uploads/2020/09/ABOUT-Card3-Our-Capabilities-And-Expertise-Filtered20.jpg)
![citizenship-hands](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/uploads/2021/12/citizenship-hands.jpg)
Tag
###  Citizenship 
####  Our role in society is underpinned by four key pillars 
These include Education and Skills Development; Inclusive Financing; Environmental Sustainability and Promoting a Just Society. Through these pillars we hope to impact as many beneficiaries as possible with the sole purpose of fighting for the eradication of unemployment, poverty and all social ills that affects communities.
[ Learn More ](https://cib.absa.africa/citizenship/)
###  Executive Leadership 
####  Zaid joined Absa Group on 1 December 2025 and was appointed Chief Executive, Corporate and Investment Banking on 1 January 2026. 
Zaid has over 20 years of experience in corporate and investment banking across Africa. Recognised for driving client excellence, growth and innovation, he has led high performing teams within various divisions and advised clients across all sectors to achieve their strategic objectives. Zaid joined Standard Bank in 2003 and held senior leadership roles including Head of Client Coverage South Africa, Head of CIB South Africa and Head of Global Markets, CIB, where he transformed client engagement, strengthened market leadership and delivered sustainable value creation.
His career demonstrates a proven ability to embed client centric models, execute landmark transactions and lead with impact.
Qualifications: B Com and Dip Acc Honours from the University of Natal; CA (SA); Advanced Management Programme (INSEAD Business School).
[ Learn More ](https://www.absa.africa/about-us/board-and-management/)
![Zaid-Moola-resized](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Zaid-Moola-resized.jpg)
![Themba-616X579_2](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/uploads/2026/06/Themba-616X579_2.jpg)
Tag
###  Executive Leadership 
####  Themba Rikhotso - Managing Executive: Transactional Banking, Absa Corporate and Investment Banking 
Themba Rikhotso brings with over 2 decades of experience in financial services with deep expertise in sustainable development finance, transactional banking, business development, business transformation, stakeholder management, and senior leadership across multiple geographies. Recently he has served as Chief Executive Officer of the Land and Agriculture Development Bank of South Africa (also known as Land Bank of South) from April 2023 to April 2026. During his tenure at the Land Bank, Themba led a significant transformation of the bank, and strengthened operational performance, brand reputation, and governance framework in a complex and demanding environment.
Themba holds a Master of Business Leadership degree from University of South Africa, and Bachelor of Commerce degree from University of Kwa-Zulu Natal. He has also completed an Executive Development Program from Wharton Business School, Executive Development Program from MIT, and an International Development Program from GIBS.
###  Executive Leadership 
####  Clive Potter: Managing Executive: Client Coverage, Absa Corporate and Investment Banking 
Clive joined Absa Group on30 March 2026 as Managing Executive: Client Coverage, Corporate and Investment Banking. Clive has over 20 years of experience in Corporate and Investment banking across South Africa, Africa and various International markets. Known for a deeply client-led strategic approach, he has an exceptional track record of embedding client-centric models, driving collaboration across platforms and supporting sustainable growth.
His experience spans Investment Banking, Global Markets, Leveraged Finance, Corporate and Transactional Banking, and Wealth Management. His career demonstrates an exceptional track record of cultivating trusted executive and board-level relationships and originating transformational mandates for Global Multinational Corporates and large local organisations.
Qualifications: University of the Witwatersrand; CFA Institute; Harvard Business School; INSEAD
![EXCO_616X579](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/uploads/2026/06/EXCO_616X579.jpg)

### [Dangote Cement Deal](https://cib.absa.africa/deals/dangote-cement-deal/ "Dangote Cement Deal")
The Absa Nigeria team acted as Joint Lead on the Dangote Cement Plc Deal, allocating NGN 116 billion across a 5-, 7-, and 10-year fixed-rate deal.   
  
The bravery to imagine. That’s Africanacity.

We are proud to have acted as the Joint Mandated Lead Arranger for Air Liquide's R5.9 billion where we refinanced a portion of the acquisition of Sasol's air separation units located in Secunda, South Africa. This is the biggest oxygen production site in the world.   
  
The bravery to imagine. That’s Africanacity.   
  
[Explore the deal](https://cib.absa.africa/home/insights-and-events/funding-solutions-as-abundant-as-the-air-that-we-breathe/)
[More](https://cib.absa.africa/deals/air-liquide-deal/)

Absa advised IHS on the acquisition, and sale and leaseback of 5,709 telecommunication towers from MTN in South Africa in a deal worth R6,4 billion. Through this transaction, IHS will enter South Africa and become the largest independent tower company in the country. The bravery to imagine. That’s Africanacity. #  Taking business to more   
of Africa than ever before
[Absa | Corporate and Investment Banking](https://cib.absa.africa "Go to Absa | Corporate and Investment Banking.") > [About Us](https://cib.absa.africa/about-us/ "Go to About Us.") > Taking business to more of Africa than ever before
![Absa-CIB-Author](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Absa-CIB-Author.png)
### Absa CIB Admin
#####  SHARE
[![Facebook](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/plugins/ultimate-social-media-icons/images/icons_theme/thin/thin_facebook.png)](https://www.facebook.com/AbsaSouthAfrica)
[![Twitter](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/plugins/ultimate-social-media-icons/images/icons_theme/thin/thin_twitter.png)](https://twitter.com/AbsaSouthAfrica)
[![](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/plugins/ultimate-social-media-icons/images/icons_theme/thin/thin_linkedin.png)](https://www.linkedin.com/company/absa)
_Absa and Société Générale: Taking business to more of Africa than ever before_
In January 2019, a Memorandum of Understanding was signed between Absa and Société Générale (SocGen). Since then, a detailed cooperation agreement has been established, covering [Transactional Banking](https://cib.absa.africa/home/insights-and-events/expert-solutions-for-your-transactional-banking-needs/) , including Trade Finance, Cash Management and Client Coverage.
The collaboration with SocGen creates a unique African proposition whose benefits include:
  * A combined broad presence across 27 African countries.
  * A single entry point for client referrals and queries,
  * A simplified engagement through international expertise with local knowledge and proximity.
  * An opportunity to support our clients' pan-African activity, with innovative digital capability across multiple sectors and geographies.
  * Global expertise that enables us to drive connectivity across key client corridors of UK/Europe, US & China, into and within Africa.


The agreement is in line with Absa's growth strategy which aims to further develop its wholesale banking activities and extend its reach into key African trading corridors. It is also aligned with SocGen's growth ambition in Africa: to further strengthen its client coverage on the continent and foster its dynamic local growth strategy.
Ultimately, this innovative approach, driven by a shared ambition in Africa, has enabled both parties to better serve clients, both local and international, across the African continent.

#  Taking business to more   
of Africa than ever before
[Absa | Corporate and Investment Banking](https://cib.absa.africa "Go to Absa | Corporate and Investment Banking.") > [About Us](https://cib.absa.africa/about-us/ "Go to About Us.") > Taking business to more of Africa than ever before
![Absa-CIB-Author](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Absa-CIB-Author.png)
### Absa CIB Admin
#####  SHARE
[![Facebook](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/plugins/ultimate-social-media-icons/images/icons_theme/thin/thin_facebook.png)](https://www.facebook.com/AbsaSouthAfrica)
[![Twitter](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/plugins/ultimate-social-media-icons/images/icons_theme/thin/thin_twitter.png)](https://twitter.com/AbsaSouthAfrica)
[![](https://cib.absa.africa/wp-content/plugins/ultimate-social-media-icons/images/icons_theme/thin/thin_linkedin.png)](https://www.linkedin.com/company/absa)
_Absa and Société Générale: Taking business to more of Africa than ever before_
In January 2019, a Memorandum of Understanding was signed between Absa and Société Générale (SocGen). Since then, a detailed cooperation agreement has been established, covering [Transactional Banking](https://cib.absa.africa/home/insights-and-events/expert-solutions-for-your-transactional-banking-needs/) , including Trade Finance, Cash Management and Client Coverage.
The collaboration with SocGen creates a unique African proposition whose benefits include:
  * A combined broad presence across 27 African countries.
  * A single entry point for client referrals and queries,
  * A simplified engagement through international expertise with local knowledge and proximity.
  * An opportunity to support our clients' pan-African activity, with innovative digital capability across multiple sectors and geographies.
  * Global expertise that enables us to drive connectivity across key client corridors of UK/Europe, US & China, into and within Africa.


The agreement is in line with Absa's growth strategy which aims to further develop its wholesale banking activities and extend its reach into key African trading corridors. It is also aligned with SocGen's growth ambition in Africa: to further strengthen its client coverage on the continent and foster its dynamic local growth strategy.
Ultimately, this innovative approach, driven by a shared ambition in Africa, has enabled both parties to better serve clients, both local and international, across the African continent.
